### Example 1
Rule:
You can pick-up color1. You can stack color1 on-top-of color2. You can stack color1 on-top-of table.

Init state:
<blue>
<yellow>
<red on green>

Goal state:
<blue on green on yellow>
<red>

Plan:
step 1: pick-up red
step 2: stack red on-top-of table
step 3: pick-up green
step 4: stack green on-top-of yellow
step 5: pick-up blue
step 6: stack blue on-top-of green
